 saath hi desh ke sabhi bank (sarkari or privet) apni sabhi branch ko is kaam ko karne ke liye taiyaar karen
 But is your bank ready for this responsibility? Does he have all the facilities available so that he can do this work well? The Reserve Bank of India is the central bank of the country
 bainkon kaa bank yaa kahen sarkaar kaa bank
 Printing of new currency is the responsibility of the Reserve Bank
 maujuuda samay main 2000 rupye, 500 rupye or 100 rupye kii karency kii printing kaa kaam bina ruke chal rahaa he
 As soon as the printing of incurrence in the printing press of RBI is completed, they are sent to all the banks of the country

 is list main shaamil bank karency chest se las rahete hai

 Vodafone ne bharat main 158 rupee kaa ek nayaa preeped plan launch kiya he
 Vodafone has launched this 158-rupee plan in Kerala circle
 is plan main graahakon ko analimited wais kol ke saath pratidin 1GB data milegaa
 However, customers will not get the benefit of SMS in this plan
 philhal is plan ko kisi duusare cirkil ke liye pesh nahin kiya gaya he
 It is expected that it will be launched in other circles soon
 158 rupeemen milane vaale kul phaaydon ke bare main baat karen to ab isamen local / STD analimited wais kol, roming kol or pratidin 1GB data diya jayega
 The validity of this plan will be 28 days
 saath hi kol kii limit pratidin 250 minute or prati hafte 1000 minute kii hogi
 Apart from this, the company has also launched another prepaid plan of Rs 151 in Kerala Circle itself
 isamen analimited kol, roming kol or keval 1GB data diya jayega
 The validity of this plan is also 28 days only
 isse pehle pichley maheene ke ant main vodaphone ne telecom sector main jeeyo or airtel se mukaable ke bich 198 rupee vaale plan main badlaav kiya tha
 Now 1 per day in this prepaid plan
 4GB data diya jayega
 In addition, unlimited local and STD calls, roaming calls and 100SMS per day will also be given in this pack
